\normalsize%
\section{$\mathfrak{sp}_{4}$}%
\section*{For $n=2$, our goal is to have $r(\sigma) \cdot \delta(\sigma) \leq 2n^2 = 8 \quad \forall \sigma$.}%

%
\linebreak%

    \begin{center}
    \label{table:sp_4}
    \begin{longtable}{||c|c|c|c|c||}
    \caption{$r(\sigma)$ and $\delta(\sigma)$ for representations $\sigma: \mathfrak{sl}_2 \to \mathfrak{sp}_{4}$}
    \hline
    Partition $\textbf{d}_\sigma$
    &indices of maximal $r_i(\sigma)$
    &$r(\sigma)$
    &$\delta(\sigma)$
    &$r(\sigma) \cdot \delta(\sigma)$
    \\ [0.3ex] \hline\endhead
    $[4]$ & NA & $\infty$ & $0$ & NA \\ \hline 
$[2^{2}]$ & $[2]$ & $4$ & $0$ & $0$ \\ \hline 
$[2, 1^{2}]$ & $[1]$ & $3$ & $1$ & $3$ \\ \hline 
$[1^{4}]$ & $[1, 2]$ & $2$ & $4$ & $8$ \\ \hline 
    \end{longtable}
    \end{center}
    %
\newpage
